{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01H8jsJussdAcxYv2KnC1jwH","type":"tool_result","content":"{\"content\":\"1: // SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0\\n2: // Copyright Authors of Cilium\\n3: \\n4: package resource\\n5: \\n6: import (\\n7: \\t\\\"context\\\"\\n8: \\t\\\"fmt\\\"\\n9: \\t\\\"reflect\\\"\\n10: \\t\\\"runtime\\\"\\n11: \\t\\\"strconv\\\"\\n12: \\t\\\"strings\\\"\\n13: \\t\\\"sync\\\"\\n14: \\n15: \\t\\\"github.com/cilium/hive/cell\\\"\\n16: \\t\\\"github.com/cilium/stream\\\"\\n17: \\tcorev1 \\\"k8s.io/api/core/v1\\\"\\n18: \\t\\\"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/meta\\\"\\n19: \\tk8sRuntime \\\"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime\\\"\\n20: \\t\\\"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types\\\"\\n21: \\t\\\"k8s.io/client-go/tools/cache\\\"\\n22: \\t\\\"k8s.io/client-go/util/workqueue\\\"\\n23: \\t\\\"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client/apiutil\\\"\\n24: \\n25: \\tk8smetrics \\\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/metrics\\\"\\n26: \\t\\\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/synced\\\"\\n27: \\t\\\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/watchers/resources\\\"\\n28: \\t\\\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock\\\"\\n29: \\t\\\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/metrics\\\"\\n30: \\t\\\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/promise\\\"\\n31: )\\n32: \\n33: // Resource provides access to a Kubernetes resource through either\\n34: // a stream of events or a read-only store.\\n35: //\\n36: // Observing of the events can be done from a constructor as subscriber\\n37: // registration is non-blocking.\\n38: //\\n39: // Store() however should only be called from a start hook, or from a\\n40: // goroutine forked from the start hook as it blocks until the store\\n41: // has been synchronized.\\n42: //\\n43: // The subscriber can process the events from Events() asynchronously and in\\n44: // parallel, but for each event the Done() function must be called to mark\\n45: // the event as handled. If not done no new events will be emitted for this key.\\n46: // If an event handling is marked as failed the configured error handler is called\\n47: // (WithErrorHandler). The default error handler will requeue the event (by its key) for\\n48: // later retried processing. The requeueing is rate limited and can be configured with\\n49: // WithRateLimiter option to Events().\\n50: //\\n51: // The resource is lazy, e.g. it will not start the informer until a call\\n52: // has been made to Events() or Store().\\n53: type Resource[T k8sRuntime.Object] interface {\\n54: \\t// Resource can be observed either via Observe() or via Events(). The observable\\n55: \\t// is implemented in terms of Events() and same semantics apply.\\n56: \\tstream.Observable[Event[T]]\\n57: \\n58: \\t// Events returns a channel of events. Each event must be marked as handled\\n59: \\t// with a call to Done() which marks the key processed. No new events for this key\\n60: \\t// will be emitted before Done() is called.\\n61: \\t//\\n62: \\t// A missing Done() will lead to an eventual panic (via finalizer on Event[T]).\\n63: \\t// Panic on this situation is needed as otherwise no new events would be emitted\\n64: \\t// and thus this needs to be enforced.\\n65: \\t//\\n66: \\t// A stream of Upsert events are emitted first to replay the current state of the\\n67: \\t// store after which incremental upserts and deletes follow until the underlying\\n68: \\t// store is synchronized after which a Sync event is emitted and further incremental\\n69: \\t// updates:\\n70: \\t//\\n71: \\t//\\t(start observing), Upsert, Upsert, Upsert, (done replaying store contents), Upsert, Upsert,\\n72: \\t//\\t  (store synchronized with API server), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\\n73: \\t//\\n74: \\t// The emitting of the Sync event does not depend on whether or not Upsert events have\\n75: \\t// all been marked Done() without an error. The sync event solely signals that the underlying\\n76: \\t// store has synchronized and that Upsert events for objects in a synchronized store have been\\n77: \\t// sent to the observer.\\n78: \\t//\\n79: \\t// When Done() is called with non-nil error the error handler is invoked, which\\n80: \\t// can ignore, requeue the event (by key) or close the channel. cnp.GetNamespace()\n\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tswitch event.Kind {\n\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t// Increment the policy count for this policy count for this namespace\n\t\tif count, exists := c.policyCountByNamespace[namespace]; exists && count > 0 {\n\t\t\tc.policyCountByNamespace[namespace]--\n\t\t}\n\t\tc.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\t\"namespace\":      namespace,\n\t\t\t\"policy\":         cnp.GetName(),\n\t\t\t\"policyCount\":    c.policyCountByNamespace[namespace],\n\t\t\tlogfields.LogSubsys: \"policy-quota-controller\",\n\t\t}).Debug(\"CiliumNetworkPolicy deleted\")\n\n\tcase resource.Sync:\n\t\t// Sync event signals that quota.Spec.MaxPoliciesPerNamespace,\n\t\t\tlogfields.LogSubsys: \"policy-quota-controller\",\n\t\t}).Debug(\"CiliumPolicyQuota created/updated\")\n\n\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t// Remove the quota\n\t\tdelete(c.quotaByNamespace, quota.Name)\n\t\tc.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\t\"quotaName\":        quota.Name,\n\t\t\tlogfields.LogSubsys: quota,\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// GetPolicyCounts returns a copy of the current policy counts per namespace (for testing/debugging)\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) Main Run Loop (controller.go)\n\n```go\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n    c.logger.Info(\"Starting PolicyQuotaController\")\n    \n    cnpEvents := c.ciliumNetworkPolicies.Events(ctx)\n    quotaEvents := c.policyQuota.Events(ctx)\n    \n    for {\n        select {\n        case <-ctx.Done():\n            return ctx.Err()\n            \n        case event, ok := <-cnpEvents:\n            if !ok {\n                cnpEvents = nil\n                break\n            }\n            c.handleCNPEvent(event)  // Updates policy counts\n            \n        case event, ok := <-quotaEvents:\n            if !ok {\n                quotaEvents = nil\n                break\n            }\n            c.handleQuotaEvent(event)  // Updates quota definitions\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## 4. Quota Checking (controller.go)\n\n```go\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n    c.mu.RLock()\n    defer c.mu.RUnlock()\n    \n    if quota, exists := c.quotaByNamespace[namespace]; exists {\n        currentCount := c.policyCountByNamespace[namespace]\n        if currentCount >= quota {\n            return fmt.Errorf(\n                \"policy quota exceeded for namespace %q: current=%d, max=%d\",\n                namespace, currentCount, quota,\n            )\n        }\n    }\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n## 5. Event Handling (controller.go)\n\n```go\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) handleCNPEvent(\n    event resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n) {\n    defer event.Done(nil)  // Proper lifecycle management\n    \n    cnp := event.Object\n    if cnp == nil {\n        return\n    }\n    \n    namespace := cnp.GetNamespace()\n    c.mu.Lock()\n    defer c.mu.Unlock()\n    \n    switch event.Kind {\n    case resource.Upsert:\n        c.policyCountByNamespace[namespace]++\n        c.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n            \"namespace\":      namespace,\n            \"policy\":         cnp.GetName(),\n            \"policyCount\":    c.policyCountByNamespace[namespace],\n            logfields.LogSubsys: \"policy-quota-controller\",\n        }).Debug(\"CiliumNetworkPolicy created/updated\")\n        \n    case resource.Delete:\n        if count, exists := c.policyCountByNamespace[namespace]; exists && count > 0 {\n            c.policyCountByNamespace[namespace]--\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## 6. Test Coverage (controller_test.go)\n\n```go\nfunc TestCheckQuotaExceeded(t *testing.T) {\n    controller := NewPolicyQuotaController(cnpResource, quotaResource)\n    \n    // Set up quota and policy count\n    controller.quotaByNamespace[\"default\"] = 5\n    controller.policyCountByNamespace[\"default\"] = 5\n    \n    // Should return error when at limit\n    err := controller.CheckQuota(\"default\")\n    assert.Error(t, err)\n    assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), \"policy quota exceeded\")\n    assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), \"default\")\n}\n\nfunc TestConcurrentAccess(t *testing.T) {\n    controller := NewPolicyQuotaController(cnpResource, quotaResource)\n    done := make(chan bool, 20)\n    \n    // Launch 20 concurrent goroutines\n    for i := 0; i < 10; i++ {\n        go func() {\n            _ = controller.CheckQuota(\"default\")\n            done <- true\n        }()\n    }\n    \n    for i := 0; i < 10; i++ {\n        go func() {\n            _ = controller.GetPolicyCounts()\n            _ = controller.GetQuotas()\n            done <- true\n        }()\n    }\n    \n    // Verify all complete without race conditions\n    for i := 0; i < 20; i++ {\n        <-done\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## 7.
